function setLang(lang) {
currentLang = lang;
document.getElementById(&#39;btnFr&#39;).classList.toggle(&#39;active&#39;, lang === &#39;fr&#39;);
document.getElementById(&#39;btnEn&#39;).classList.toggle(&#39;active&#39;, lang === &#39;en&#39;);
document.getElementById(&#39;title&#39;).textContent = t(&#39;title&#39;);
document.getElementById(&#39;lblPopulation&#39;).textContent = t(&#39;population&#39;);
document.querySelector(&#39;#regenerateBtn span&#39;).textContent = t(&#39;regenerate&#39;);
document.querySelector(&#39;#randomSeedBtn span&#39;).textContent = t(&#39;randomSeed&#39;);
render();
}

let malePhotos = [];
let femalePhotos = [];
let photosLoaded = false;
let malePhotosSeed = [];
let femalePhotosSeed = [];

function gdUrl(id) { return `https://drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=${id}&amp;sz=w200`; }

async function loadPhotos() {
malePhotos = GDRIVE_PHOTOS.hommes.map(gdUrl);
femalePhotos = GDRIVE_PHOTOS.femmes.map(gdUrl);
photosLoaded = true;
shufflePhotosWithSeed();
}

function shufflePhotosWithSeed() {
const rng = mulberry32(baseSeed + 999999);
malePhotosSeed = [...malePhotos];
femalePhotosSeed = [...femalePhotos];
for (let i = malePhotosSeed.length - 1; i &gt; 0; i--) { const j = Math.floor(rng() * (i + 1)); [malePhotosSeed[i], malePhotosSeed[j]] = [malePhotosSeed[j], malePhotosSeed[i]]; }
for (let i = femalePhotosSeed.length - 1; i &gt; 0; i--) { const j = Math.floor(rng() * (i + 1)); [femalePhotosSeed[i], femalePhotosSeed[j]] = [femalePhotosSeed[j], femalePhotosSeed[i]]; }
}

function getPhotoUrl(person) {
const photos = person.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? malePhotosSeed : femalePhotosSeed;
if (!photos.length) return null;
const rng = mulberry32(baseSeed ^ (person.id * 2654435761));
const idx = Math.floor(rng() * photos.length);
return photos[idx];
}

function mulberry32(a) {
return function() {
let t = a += 0x6D2B79F5;
t = Math.imul(t ^ t &gt;&gt;&gt; 15, t | 1);
t ^= t + Math.imul(t ^ t &gt;&gt;&gt; 7, t | 61);
return ((t ^ t &gt;&gt;&gt; 14) &gt;&gt;&gt; 0) / 4294967296;
}
}

function getImpactAndCarrure(forTai) {
if (forTai &lt;= 64) return { bd: &quot;-2&quot;, carrure: -2 };
if (forTai &lt;= 84) return { bd: &quot;-1&quot;, carrure: -1 };
if (forTai &lt;= 124) return { bd: &quot;Aucun&quot;, carrure: 0 };
if (forTai &lt;= 164) return { bd: &quot;+1D4&quot;, carrure: 1 };
if (forTai &lt;= 204) return { bd: &quot;+1D6&quot;, carrure: 2 };
if (forTai &lt;= 284) return { bd: &quot;+2D6&quot;, carrure: 3 };
if (forTai &lt;= 364) return { bd: &quot;+3D6&quot;, carrure: 4 };
if (forTai &lt;= 444) return { bd: &quot;+4D6&quot;, carrure: 5 };
return { bd: &quot;+5D6&quot;, carrure: 6 };
}

function generateCthulhuStats(person, rng) {
const profile = jobSkillProfiles[person.job] || jobSkillProfiles[&quot;_default&quot;];
const bonus = profile.statBonus || {};
const roll3d6x5 = () =&gt; (Math.floor(rng() * 6) + Math.floor(rng() * 6) + Math.floor(rng() * 6) + 3) * 5;
const roll2d6p6x5 = () =&gt; (Math.floor(rng() * 6) + Math.floor(rng() * 6) + 8) * 5;
let FOR = roll3d6x5() + (bonus.FOR || 0);
let CON = roll3d6x5() + (bonus.CON || 0);
let DEX = roll3d6x5() + (bonus.DEX || 0);
let TAI = roll2d6p6x5();
let INT = roll2d6p6x5() + (bonus.INT || 0);
let POU = roll3d6x5() + (bonus.POU || 0);
let APP = roll3d6x5() + (bonus.APP || 0);
let EDU = roll2d6p6x5() + (bonus.EDU || 0);
if (person.age &lt; 20) { EDU = Math.max(30, EDU - 10); }
else if (person.age &gt;= 40 &amp;&amp; person.age &lt; 50) { EDU += 5; const loss = (Math.floor(rng() * 3) + 1) * 5; if (rng() &gt; 0.5) FOR = Math.max(15, FOR - loss); else CON = Math.max(15, CON - loss); }
else if (person.age &gt;= 50 &amp;&amp; person.age &lt; 60) { EDU += 10; FOR = Math.max(15, FOR - 10); CON = Math.max(15, CON - 10); DEX = Math.max(15, DEX - 5); APP = Math.max(15, APP - 5); }
else if (person.age &gt;= 60) { EDU += 15; FOR = Math.max(15, FOR - 20); CON = Math.max(15, CON - 20); DEX = Math.max(15, DEX - 15); APP = Math.max(15, APP - 15); }
FOR = Math.min(90, Math.max(15, FOR)); CON = Math.min(90, Math.max(15, CON));
DEX = Math.min(90, Math.max(15, DEX)); TAI = Math.min(90, Math.max(40, TAI));
INT = Math.min(90, Math.max(40, INT)); POU = Math.min(90, Math.max(15, POU));
APP = Math.min(90, Math.max(15, APP)); EDU = Math.min(99, Math.max(30, EDU));
const { bd: BD, carrure: CARRURE } = getImpactAndCarrure(FOR + TAI);
const SAN = POU; const PV = Math.floor((CON + TAI) / 10);
const PM = Math.floor(POU / 5); const CHANCE = 15 + Math.floor(rng() * 51);
let MVT = 8;
if (FOR &lt; TAI &amp;&amp; DEX &lt; TAI) MVT = 7; else if (FOR &gt; TAI &amp;&amp; DEX &gt; TAI) MVT = 9;
if (person.age &gt;= 40 &amp;&amp; person.age &lt; 50) MVT = Math.max(1, MVT - 1);
else if (person.age &gt;= 50 &amp;&amp; person.age &lt; 60) MVT = Math.max(1, MVT - 2);
else if (person.age &gt;= 60 &amp;&amp; person.age &lt; 70) MVT = Math.max(1, MVT - 3);
else if (person.age &gt;= 70) MVT = Math.max(1, MVT - 4);
const skills = {};
skills[&quot;Langue maternelle&quot;] = Math.min(99, EDU);
skills[&quot;Esquive&quot;] = Math.floor(DEX / 2);
for (const [skillName, range] of Object.entries(profile.skills || {})) {
skills[skillName] = Math.floor(rng() * (range[1] - range[0] + 1)) + range[0];
}
const creditRange = profile.credit || [5, 20];
skills[&quot;Crédit&quot;] = Math.floor(rng() * (creditRange[1] - creditRange[0] + 1)) + creditRange[0];
const allSkills = Object.keys(skillsBase).filter(s =&gt; !skills[s] &amp;&amp; s !== &quot;Mythe de Cthulhu&quot; &amp;&amp; s !== &quot;Esquive&quot; &amp;&amp; s !== &quot;Langue maternelle&quot; &amp;&amp; s !== &quot;Crédit&quot;);
const numHobbies = 2 + Math.floor(rng() * 3);
for (let i = 0; i &lt; numHobbies &amp;&amp; allSkills.length &gt; 0; i++) {
const idx = Math.floor(rng() * allSkills.length);
const hobby = allSkills.splice(idx, 1)[0];
skills[hobby] = (skillsBase[hobby] || 1) + Math.floor(rng() * 25) + 10;
}
const weapons = [];
for (const weaponName of (profile.weapons || [&quot;Poing&quot;])) {
const weapon = weaponsList.find(w =&gt; w.name === weaponName);
if (!weapon) continue;
let baseSkill = 25;
if (weaponName.includes(&quot;Revolver&quot;) || weaponName.includes(&quot;Automatique&quot;) || weaponName.includes(&quot;Derringer&quot;)) baseSkill = skills[&quot;Combat. Arme à feu (Armes de poing)&quot;] || 20;
else if (weaponName.includes(&quot;Fusil&quot;) || weaponName.includes(&quot;Carabine&quot;)) baseSkill = skills[&quot;Combat. Arme à feu (Fusils)&quot;] || 25;
else if (weaponName.includes(&quot;Thompson&quot;)) baseSkill = skills[&quot;Combat. Arme à feu (Mitraillettes)&quot;] || 15;
else if (weaponName === &quot;Hache&quot; || weaponName === &quot;Pioche&quot;) baseSkill = skills[&quot;Combat. Au Contact (Haches)&quot;] || 15;
else baseSkill = skills[&quot;Combat. Au Contact (Corps à corps)&quot;] || 25;
const finalSkill = Math.min(85, baseSkill + Math.floor(rng() * 15) + 5);
let damage = weapon.damage;
if (damage.includes(&quot;BD&quot;)) { if (BD === &quot;Aucun&quot;) damage = damage.replace(&quot;+BD&quot;, &quot;&quot;).replace(&quot;BD&quot;, &quot;&quot;); else damage = damage.replace(&quot;BD&quot;, BD); }
weapons.push({ name: weapon.name, skill: finalSkill, damage });
}
return { FOR, CON, DEX, TAI, INT, POU, APP, EDU, SAN, PV, PM, BD, CARRURE, MVT, CHANCE, skills, weapons };
}

function formatStatsForFoundry(person, stats) {
const name = getPersonName(person);
const en = currentLang === &#39;en&#39;;
const ageLabel = en ? `age ${person.age}` : `${person.age} ans`;
let text = `${name}, ${ageLabel}\n`;
if (en) {
text += `STR ${stats.FOR} CON ${stats.CON} SIZ ${stats.TAI} DEX ${stats.DEX} APP ${stats.APP} INT ${stats.INT}\n`;
text += `POW ${stats.POU} EDU ${stats.EDU} SAN ${stats.SAN} HP ${stats.PV} DB: ${stats.BD}\n`;
text += `Build: ${stats.CARRURE} Move: ${stats.MVT} MP: ${stats.PM} Luck: ${stats.CHANCE}\n\n`;
} else {
text += `FOR ${stats.FOR} CON ${stats.CON} TAI ${stats.TAI} DEX ${stats.DEX} APP ${stats.APP} INT ${stats.INT}\n`;
text += `POU ${stats.POU} ÉDU ${stats.EDU} SAN ${stats.SAN} PV ${stats.PV} BD: ${stats.BD}\n`;
text += `Carrure: ${stats.CARRURE} Mvt: ${stats.MVT} PM: ${stats.PM} Chance: ${stats.CHANCE}\n\n`;
}
if (stats.weapons.length &gt; 0) {
text += en ? `Combat\n` : `Attaques\n`;
for (const w of stats.weapons) {
const half = Math.floor(w.skill / 2); const fifth = Math.floor(w.skill / 5);
const wName = en ? tWeapon(w.name) : w.name;
const dmgLabel = en ? `damage` : `dommage`;
text += `${wName} ${w.skill}% (${half}/${fifth}), ${dmgLabel} ${w.damage}\n`;
}
const esq = stats.skills[&quot;Esquive&quot;] || Math.floor(stats.DEX / 2);
const dodgeLabel = en ? `Dodge` : `Esquiver`;
text += `${dodgeLabel} ${esq}% (${Math.floor(esq/2)}/${Math.floor(esq/5)})\n\n`;
}
text += en ? `Skills\n` : `Compétences\n`;
const sorted = Object.entries(stats.skills).filter(([n]) =&gt; n !== &quot;Esquive&quot; &amp;&amp; n !== &quot;Crédit&quot;).sort((a, b) =&gt; a[0].localeCompare(b[0]));
const langSkills = sorted.filter(([n]) =&gt; n.startsWith(&quot;Langue&quot;));
const otherSkills = sorted.filter(([n]) =&gt; !n.startsWith(&quot;Langue&quot;));
text += otherSkills.map(([n, v]) =&gt; `${en ? tSkill(n) : n} ${v}%`).join(&quot;, &quot;);
if (langSkills.length &gt; 0) {
text += `\n${en ? &#39;Languages&#39; : &#39;Langues&#39;}: ` + langSkills.map(([n, v]) =&gt; `${en ? tSkill(n) : n} ${v}%`).join(&quot;, &quot;) + &quot;.&quot;;
}
return text;
}

function sliderToPopulation(v) {
if (v &lt;= 500) return Math.max(1, Math.round(v * 10));
const t = (v - 500) / 500;
return Math.round(5000 * Math.pow(1000, t));
}
function populationToSlider(p) {
if (p &lt;= 5000) return Math.round(p / 10);
const t = Math.log(p / 5000) / Math.log(1000);
return Math.round(500 + t * 500);
}

async function generatePopulation() {
totalPopulation = parseInt(document.getElementById(&#39;popInput&#39;).value) || 1;
const showProgress = totalPopulation &gt; 10000;
const generating = document.getElementById(&#39;generating&#39;);
const progressFill = document.getElementById(&#39;progressFill&#39;);
const progressText = document.getElementById(&#39;progressText&#39;);
if (showProgress) { generating.classList.add(&#39;active&#39;); progressFill.style.width = &#39;0%&#39;; progressText.textContent = t(&#39;initProgress&#39;); await new Promise(r =&gt; setTimeout(r, 10)); }
const rng = mulberry32(baseSeed);
people = []; jobIndex = {};
const jobCounts = {};
for (const cat of Object.values(cthulhuData.jobs)) {
for (const job of cat.jobs) {
if (totalPopulation &gt;= job.threshold) {
jobCounts[job.name] = Math.max(1, Math.floor(totalPopulation * job.ratio));
jobIndex[job.name] = [];
}
}
}
if (showProgress) { progressText.textContent = t(&#39;familyProgress&#39;); progressFill.style.width = &#39;10%&#39;; await new Promise(r =&gt; setTimeout(r, 10)); }
let personId = 0; let remaining = totalPopulation;
while (remaining &gt; 0) {
const familySize = Math.min(remaining, Math.floor(rng() * 5) + 2);
const lastNameIdx = Math.floor(rng() * cthulhuData.lastNames.length);
let parent1Id = null, parent2Id = null;
const isSeniorFamily = rng() &lt; 0.08;
const p1Age = isSeniorFamily ? Math.floor(rng() * 26) + 65 : Math.floor(rng() * 35) + 30;
const isGayCouple = rng() &lt; 0.03;
const p1Gender = rng() &gt; 0.5 ? &#39;male&#39; : &#39;female&#39;;
const p1NameIdx = Math.floor(rng() * (p1Gender === &#39;male&#39; ? cthulhuData.firstNamesMale : cthulhuData.firstNamesFemale).length);
people.push({ id: personId, firstNameIdx: p1NameIdx, lastNameIdx, gender: p1Gender, age: p1Age, job: null, spouseId: null, childrenIds: [], parentIds: [], siblingIds: [], isGay: isGayCouple });
parent1Id = personId++;
remaining--;
if (remaining &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; rng() &gt; 0.15) {
const p2Age = Math.max(18, p1Age + Math.floor(rng() * 10) - 5);
const p2Gender = isGayCouple ? p1Gender : (p1Gender === &#39;male&#39; ? &#39;female&#39; : &#39;male&#39;);
const p2NameIdx = Math.floor(rng() * (p2Gender === &#39;male&#39; ? cthulhuData.firstNamesMale : cthulhuData.firstNamesFemale).length);
people.push({ id: personId, firstNameIdx: p2NameIdx, lastNameIdx, gender: p2Gender, age: p2Age, job: null, spouseId: parent1Id, childrenIds: [], parentIds: [], siblingIds: [], isGay: isGayCouple });
parent2Id = personId++;
people[parent1Id].spouseId = parent2Id;
remaining--;
}
const numChildren = Math.min(remaining, Math.max(0, familySize - (parent2Id !== null ? 2 : 1)));
const childrenIds = [];
for (let i = 0; i &lt; numChildren; i++) {
const childGender = rng() &gt; 0.5 ? &#39;male&#39; : &#39;female&#39;;
const childAge = Math.max(1, p1Age - 18 - Math.floor(rng() * 15));
const childNames = childGender === &#39;male&#39; ? cthulhuData.firstNamesMale : cthulhuData.firstNamesFemale;
const childNameIdx = Math.floor(rng() * childNames.length);
const parentIds = parent2Id !== null ? [parent1Id, parent2Id] : [parent1Id];
people.push({ id: personId, firstNameIdx: childNameIdx, lastNameIdx, gender: childGender, age: childAge, job: null, spouseId: null, childrenIds: [], parentIds, siblingIds: [], isGay: false });
childrenIds.push(personId);
people[parent1Id].childrenIds.push(personId);
if (parent2Id !== null) people[parent2Id].childrenIds.push(personId);
personId++; remaining--;
}
for (const cid of childrenIds) people[cid].siblingIds = childrenIds.filter(id =&gt; id !== cid);
}
if (showProgress) { progressFill.style.width = &#39;60%&#39;; progressText.textContent = t(&#39;jobsProgress&#39;); await new Promise(r =&gt; setTimeout(r, 10)); }

if (!jobIndex[&#39;Enfant&#39;]) jobIndex[&#39;Enfant&#39;] = [];
if (!jobIndex[&#39;Retraité&#39;]) jobIndex[&#39;Retraité&#39;] = [];
if (!jobIndex[&#39;Étudiant&#39;]) jobIndex[&#39;Étudiant&#39;] = [];
if (!jobIndex[&#39;Femme au foyer&#39;]) jobIndex[&#39;Femme au foyer&#39;] = [];

// Assign children and retirees
for (const person of people) {
if (person.age &lt; 16) { person.job = &#39;Enfant&#39;; jobIndex[&#39;Enfant&#39;].push(person.id); }
else if (person.age &gt;= 65) { person.job = &#39;Retraité&#39;; jobIndex[&#39;Retraité&#39;].push(person.id); }
}

// Students: 16-25, ~25% chance, max 5% pop
const maxStudents = Math.floor(totalPopulation * 0.05);
let studentCount = 0;
for (const person of people) {
if (person.job !== null) continue;
if (person.age &gt;= 16 &amp;&amp; person.age &lt;= 25 &amp;&amp; studentCount &lt; maxStudents &amp;&amp; rng() &lt; 0.25) {
person.job = &#39;Étudiant&#39;; jobIndex[&#39;Étudiant&#39;].push(person.id); studentCount++;
}
}

// Build job slot pools using gender ratios
// For each job, decide gender for each slot using JOB_FEMALE_RATIO
const shuffleArr = (arr) =&gt; { for (let i = arr.length - 1; i &gt; 0; i--) { const j = Math.floor(rng() * (i + 1)); [arr[i], arr[j]] = [arr[j], arr[i]]; } return arr; };

// Build gendered slot queues (shuffled)
const femaleJobSlots = [];
const maleJobSlots = [];
for (const [jobName, count] of Object.entries(jobCounts)) {
if ([&#39;Enfant&#39;, &#39;Retraité&#39;, &#39;Femme au foyer&#39;, &#39;Étudiant&#39;].includes(jobName)) continue;
const femaleRatio = JOB_FEMALE_RATIO[jobName] !== undefined ? JOB_FEMALE_RATIO[jobName] : 0.15;
const numFemale = Math.round(count * femaleRatio);
const numMale = count - numFemale;
for (let i = 0; i &lt; numFemale; i++) femaleJobSlots.push(jobName);
for (let i = 0; i &lt; numMale; i++) maleJobSlots.push(jobName);
}
shuffleArr(femaleJobSlots);
shuffleArr(maleJobSlots);

// Assign housewives: ~80% of working-age females (randomly selected)
const femaleWorkingAge = people.filter(p =&gt; p.job === null &amp;&amp; p.gender === &#39;female&#39; &amp;&amp; p.age &gt;= 16 &amp;&amp; p.age &lt; 65);
shuffleArr(femaleWorkingAge);
const numHousewives = Math.floor(femaleWorkingAge.length * 0.80);
for (let i = 0; i &lt; numHousewives; i++) {
femaleWorkingAge[i].job = &#39;Femme au foyer&#39;;
jobIndex[&#39;Femme au foyer&#39;].push(femaleWorkingAge[i].id);
}

// All working-age adults still unassigned, shuffled together
const allWorkingAdults = people.filter(p =&gt; p.job === null &amp;&amp; p.age &gt;= 16 &amp;&amp; p.age &lt; 65);
shuffleArr(allWorkingAdults);

let fSlotIdx = 0, mSlotIdx = 0;
for (const person of allWorkingAdults) {
if (person.gender === &#39;female&#39;) {
if (fSlotIdx &lt; femaleJobSlots.length) {
const job = femaleJobSlots[fSlotIdx++];
person.job = job;
if (jobIndex[job]) jobIndex[job].push(person.id);
else person.job = &#39;Sans profession&#39;;
} else {
person.job = &#39;Sans profession&#39;;
}
} else {
if (mSlotIdx &lt; maleJobSlots.length) {
const job = maleJobSlots[mSlotIdx++];
person.job = job;
if (jobIndex[job]) jobIndex[job].push(person.id);
else person.job = &#39;Sans profession&#39;;
} else {
person.job = &#39;Sans profession&#39;;
}
}
}
// Anyone remaining without a job
for (const person of people.filter(p =&gt; p.job === null)) {
person.job = &#39;Sans profession&#39;;
}

if (showProgress) { progressFill.style.width = &#39;100%&#39;; progressText.textContent = t(&#39;done&#39;); await new Promise(r =&gt; setTimeout(r, 200)); generating.classList.remove(&#39;active&#39;); }
shufflePhotosWithSeed();
render();
}

function getPersonName(p) {
const fn = p.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? cthulhuData.firstNamesMale : cthulhuData.firstNamesFemale;
return fn[p.firstNameIdx] + &#39; &#39; + cthulhuData.lastNames[p.lastNameIdx];
}

function formatNumber(n) {
if (n &gt;= 1000000) return (n/1000000).toFixed(2)+&#39;M&#39;;
if (n &gt;= 1000) return (n/1000).toFixed(1)+&#39;k&#39;;
return n.toLocaleString(&#39;fr-FR&#39;);
}

function render() {
const categoriesEl = document.getElementById(&#39;categories&#39;);
categoriesEl.innerHTML = &#39;&#39;;
for (const [catKey, category] of Object.entries(cthulhuData.jobs)) {
const catEl = document.createElement(&#39;div&#39;);
catEl.className = &#39;category&#39;;
let jobsHtml = &#39;&#39;;
const sortedJobs = [...category.jobs].sort((a,b) =&gt; (jobIndex[b.name]?.length||0) - (jobIndex[a.name]?.length||0));
for (const job of sortedJobs) {
const count = jobIndex[job.name]?.length || 0;
const active = totalPopulation &gt;= job.threshold;
if (!active &amp;&amp; count === 0) continue;
const displayName = tJob(job.name);
const displayThreshold = formatNumber(job.threshold);
jobsHtml += `&lt;div class=&quot;job ${active &amp;&amp; count &gt; 0 ? &#39;&#39; : &#39;inactive&#39;}&quot; data-job=&quot;${job.name}&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;job-name&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;${job.icon}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;${displayName}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;threshold&quot;&gt;(${displayThreshold}+)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;job-count&quot;&gt;${formatNumber(count)}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`;
}
if (!jobsHtml) continue;
const catName = tCat(category.name);
catEl.innerHTML = `&lt;h2 style=&quot;border-color: ${category.color}; color: ${category.color};&quot;&gt;${catName}&lt;/h2&gt;${jobsHtml}`;
catEl.querySelectorAll(&#39;.job:not(.inactive)&#39;).forEach(jobEl =&gt; {
jobEl.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; { const ids = jobIndex[jobEl.dataset.job]; if (ids &amp;&amp; ids.length &gt; 0) openModal(jobEl.dataset.job); });
});
categoriesEl.appendChild(catEl);
}
const children = jobIndex[&#39;Enfant&#39;]?.length || 0;
const elders = jobIndex[&#39;Retraité&#39;]?.length || 0;
document.getElementById(&#39;summary&#39;).innerHTML = `
&lt;div class=&quot;summary-item&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;value&quot;&gt;${formatNumber(totalPopulation)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;label&quot;&gt;${t(&#39;population&#39;).replace(&#39;:&#39;, &#39;&#39;)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;summary-item&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;value&quot;&gt;${formatNumber(children)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;label&quot;&gt;${t(&#39;children&#39;)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;summary-item&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;value&quot;&gt;${formatNumber(totalPopulation - children - elders)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;label&quot;&gt;${t(&#39;adults&#39;)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;summary-item&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;value&quot;&gt;${formatNumber(elders)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;label&quot;&gt;${t(&#39;elderPlural&#39;)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;summary-item&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;value&quot;&gt;${Object.keys(jobIndex).length}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;label&quot;&gt;${t(&#39;jobs&#39;)}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
`;
}

function openModal(jobName) {
currentJob = jobName; currentPage = 0;
navigationHistory = [{ type: &#39;list&#39;, job: jobName }];
document.getElementById(&#39;modalOverlay&#39;).classList.add(&#39;active&#39;);
renderJobList();
}

function makeAvatarHtml(person, size = 48, isLarge = false) {
const url = getPhotoUrl(person);
const emoji = person.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? &#39;👨&#39; : &#39;👩&#39;;
const cls = isLarge ? &#39;person-avatar-large&#39; : &#39;person-avatar&#39;;
const placeholderCls = isLarge ? &#39;person-avatar-placeholder-large&#39; : &#39;person-avatar-placeholder&#39;;
if (!url) { return `&lt;div class=&quot;${placeholderCls}&quot;&gt;${emoji}&lt;/div&gt;`; }
const fallback = `&lt;div class=&#39;${placeholderCls}&#39;&gt;${emoji}&lt;/div&gt;`;
return `&lt;img src=&quot;${url}&quot; class=&quot;${cls}&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; loading=&quot;lazy&quot; onerror=&quot;this.outerHTML=&#39;${fallback.replace(/&#39;/g, &#39;&amp;apos;&#39;)}&#39;&quot;&gt;`;
}

function renderJobList() {
const modal = document.getElementById(&#39;modal&#39;);
const ids = jobIndex[currentJob] || [];
const totalPages = Math.ceil(ids.length / PEOPLE_PER_PAGE);
const start = currentPage * PEOPLE_PER_PAGE;
const end = Math.min(start + PEOPLE_PER_PAGE, ids.length);
let peopleHtml = &#39;&#39;;
for (let i = start; i &lt; end; i++) {
const p = people[ids[i]];
const name = getPersonName(p);
const relations = [];
if (p.spouseId !== null) {
const sp = people[p.spouseId];
const spName = sp.gender === &#39;female&#39; ? cthulhuData.firstNamesFemale[sp.firstNameIdx] : cthulhuData.firstNamesMale[sp.firstNameIdx];
relations.push(`💑 ${spName}${p.isGay ? &#39; &lt;span class=&quot;badge-gay&quot;&gt;🏳️‍🌈&lt;/span&gt;&#39; : &#39;&#39;}`);
}
if (p.childrenIds.length &gt; 0) relations.push(`👶 ${p.childrenIds.length}`);
const gayBadge = p.isGay &amp;&amp; p.spouseId === null ? &#39; &lt;span class=&quot;badge-gay&quot;&gt;🏳️‍🌈&lt;/span&gt;&#39; : &#39;&#39;;
peopleHtml += `&lt;div class=&quot;person-card ${p.gender}${p.isGay ? &#39; gay&#39; : &#39;&#39;}&quot; data-person-id=&quot;${p.id}&quot;&gt;
${makeAvatarHtml(p, 48, false)}
&lt;div class=&quot;person-info&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;person-name&quot;&gt;${name}${gayBadge}&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;person-age&quot;&gt;${p.age} ${t(&#39;years&#39;)}&lt;/div&gt;
${relations.length &gt; 0 ? `&lt;div class=&quot;person-relations&quot;&gt;${relations.join(&#39; • &#39;)}&lt;/div&gt;` : &#39;&#39;}
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;`;
}
let jobIcon = &#39;👤&#39;;
for (const cat of Object.values(cthulhuData.jobs)) { const found = cat.jobs.find(j =&gt; j.name === currentJob); if (found) { jobIcon = found.icon; break; } }
const displayJobName = tJob(currentJob);
modal.innerHTML = `&lt;div class=&quot;modal-header&quot;&gt;&lt;h2&gt;${jobIcon} ${displayJobName} (${formatNumber(ids.length)})&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;button class=&quot;modal-close&quot; id=&quot;closeModal&quot;&gt;&amp;times;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;people-list&quot;&gt;${peopleHtml}&lt;/div&gt;${totalPages &gt; 1 ? `&lt;div class=&quot;pagination&quot;&gt;&lt;button id=&quot;prevPage&quot; ${currentPage === 0 ? &#39;disabled&#39; : &#39;&#39;}&gt;${t(&#39;prev&#39;)}&lt;/button&gt;&lt;span&gt;${t(&#39;page&#39;)} ${currentPage + 1} ${t(&#39;of&#39;)} ${formatNumber(totalPages)}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;button id=&quot;nextPage&quot; ${currentPage &gt;= totalPages - 1 ? &#39;disabled&#39; : &#39;&#39;}&gt;${t(&#39;next&#39;)}&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;` : &#39;&#39;}`;
document.getElementById(&#39;closeModal&#39;).addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, closeModal);
document.getElementById(&#39;prevPage&#39;)?.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; { if (currentPage &gt; 0) { currentPage--; renderJobList(); }});
document.getElementById(&#39;nextPage&#39;)?.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; { if (currentPage &lt; totalPages - 1) { currentPage++; renderJobList(); }});
modal.querySelectorAll(&#39;.person-card&#39;).forEach(card =&gt; {
card.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; { navigationHistory.push({ type: &#39;detail&#39;, personId: parseInt(card.dataset.personId) }); showPersonDetail(parseInt(card.dataset.personId)); });
});
}

function showPersonDetail(personId) {
const person = people[personId];
if (!person) return;
const modal = document.getElementById(&#39;modal&#39;);
const name = getPersonName(person);
let statsHtml = &#39;&#39;;
if (person.job !== &#39;Enfant&#39;) {
const rng = mulberry32(baseSeed + personId * 9973);
const stats = generateCthulhuStats(person, rng);
const foundryText = formatStatsForFoundry(person, stats);
statsHtml = `&lt;div class=&quot;family-section&quot;&gt;&lt;h4&gt;${t(&#39;statsTitle&#39;)}&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;stats-sheet&quot; id=&quot;statsSheet&quot;&gt;${foundryText}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;button class=&quot;copy-btn&quot; id=&quot;copyBtn&quot;&gt;${t(&#39;copyBtn&#39;)}&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`;
}
let familyHtml = &#39;&#39;;
if (person.spouseId !== null) {
const spouse = people[person.spouseId];
const spouseGayBadge = person.isGay ? &#39; 🏳️‍🌈&#39; : &#39;&#39;;
familyHtml += `&lt;div class=&quot;family-section&quot;&gt;&lt;h4&gt;${t(&#39;spouse&#39;)}${spouseGayBadge}&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;family-members&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;family-member&quot; data-person-id=&quot;${spouse.id}&quot;&gt;${spouse.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? &#39;👨&#39; : &#39;👩&#39;} ${getPersonName(spouse)} &lt;span class=&quot;relation-type&quot;&gt;(${spouse.age} ${t(&#39;years&#39;)}, ${tJob(spouse.job)})&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`;
}
if (person.parentIds.length &gt; 0) {
const parentsHtml = person.parentIds.map(id =&gt; { const p = people[id]; return `&lt;div class=&quot;family-member&quot; data-person-id=&quot;${p.id}&quot;&gt;${p.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? &#39;👨&#39; : &#39;👩&#39;} ${getPersonName(p)} &lt;span class=&quot;relation-type&quot;&gt;(${p.age} ${t(&#39;years&#39;)}, ${tJob(p.job)})&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`; }).join(&#39;&#39;);
familyHtml += `&lt;div class=&quot;family-section&quot;&gt;&lt;h4&gt;${t(&#39;parents&#39;)}&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;family-members&quot;&gt;${parentsHtml}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`;
}
if (person.siblingIds.length &gt; 0) {
const siblingsHtml = person.siblingIds.map(id =&gt; { const s = people[id]; return `&lt;div class=&quot;family-member&quot; data-person-id=&quot;${s.id}&quot;&gt;${s.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? &#39;👨&#39; : &#39;👩&#39;} ${getPersonName(s)} &lt;span class=&quot;relation-type&quot;&gt;(${s.age} ${t(&#39;years&#39;)}, ${tJob(s.job)})&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`; }).join(&#39;&#39;);
familyHtml += `&lt;div class=&quot;family-section&quot;&gt;&lt;h4&gt;${t(&#39;siblings&#39;)}&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;family-members&quot;&gt;${siblingsHtml}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`;
}
if (person.childrenIds.length &gt; 0) {
const childrenHtml = person.childrenIds.map(id =&gt; { const c = people[id]; return `&lt;div class=&quot;family-member&quot; data-person-id=&quot;${c.id}&quot;&gt;${c.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? &#39;👦&#39; : &#39;👧&#39;} ${getPersonName(c)} &lt;span class=&quot;relation-type&quot;&gt;(${c.age} ${t(&#39;years&#39;)}, ${tJob(c.job)})&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`; }).join(&#39;&#39;);
familyHtml += `&lt;div class=&quot;family-section&quot;&gt;&lt;h4&gt;${t(&#39;childrenLabel&#39;)}&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;family-members&quot;&gt;${childrenHtml}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;`;
}
if (!familyHtml &amp;&amp; !statsHtml) familyHtml = `&lt;p style=&quot;color: #888; margin-top: 1rem;&quot;&gt;${t(&#39;alone&#39;)}&lt;/p&gt;`;
let jobIcon = &#39;👤&#39;;
for (const cat of Object.values(cthulhuData.jobs)) { const found = cat.jobs.find(j =&gt; j.name === person.job); if (found) { jobIcon = found.icon; break; } }
const gayBadge = person.isGay ? &#39; &lt;span class=&quot;badge-gay&quot;&gt;🏳️‍🌈&lt;/span&gt;&#39; : &#39;&#39;;
const genderLabel = person.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? t(&#39;male&#39;) : t(&#39;female&#39;);
modal.innerHTML = `
&lt;div class=&quot;modal-header&quot;&gt;&lt;h2&gt;${person.gender === &#39;male&#39; ? &#39;👨&#39; : &#39;👩&#39;} ${name}${gayBadge}&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;button class=&quot;modal-close&quot; id=&quot;closeModal&quot;&gt;&amp;times;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;button class=&quot;back-btn&quot; id=&quot;backBtn&quot;&gt;${t(&#39;back&#39;)}&lt;/button&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;person-detail&quot;&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;person-detail-header&quot;&gt;
${makeAvatarHtml(person, 100, true)}
&lt;div class=&quot;info&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;${t(&#39;age&#39;)}:&lt;/strong&gt; ${person.age} ${t(&#39;years&#39;)}&lt;br&gt;&lt;strong&gt;${t(&#39;job&#39;)}:&lt;/strong&gt; ${jobIcon} ${tJob(person.job)}&lt;br&gt;&lt;strong&gt;${t(&#39;family&#39;)}:&lt;/strong&gt; ${cthulhuData.lastNames[person.lastNameIdx]}&lt;br&gt;&lt;strong&gt;${t(&#39;gender&#39;)}:&lt;/strong&gt; ${genderLabel}${person.isGay ? &#39; 🏳️‍🌈&#39; : &#39;&#39;}&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
${statsHtml}
${familyHtml}
&lt;/div&gt;
`;
document.getElementById(&#39;closeModal&#39;).addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, closeModal);
document.getElementById(&#39;backBtn&#39;).addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; {
navigationHistory.pop();
const prev = navigationHistory[navigationHistory.length - 1];
if (prev.type === &#39;list&#39;) renderJobList(); else showPersonDetail(prev.personId);
});
const copyBtn = document.getElementById(&#39;copyBtn&#39;);
if (copyBtn) {
copyBtn.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; {
const statsSheet = document.getElementById(&#39;statsSheet&#39;);
navigator.clipboard.writeText(statsSheet.textContent).then(() =&gt; {
copyBtn.textContent = t(&#39;copied&#39;); copyBtn.classList.add(&#39;copied&#39;);
setTimeout(() =&gt; { copyBtn.textContent = t(&#39;copyBtn&#39;); copyBtn.classList.remove(&#39;copied&#39;); }, 2000);
});
});
}
modal.querySelectorAll(&#39;.family-member&#39;).forEach(member =&gt; {
member.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; { const pid = parseInt(member.dataset.personId); navigationHistory.push({ type: &#39;detail&#39;, personId: pid }); showPersonDetail(pid); });
});
}

function closeModal() { document.getElementById(&#39;modalOverlay&#39;).classList.remove(&#39;active&#39;); currentJob = null; navigationHistory = []; }

const popSlider = document.getElementById(&#39;popSlider&#39;);
const popInput = document.getElementById(&#39;popInput&#39;);
let generateTimeout = null;
popSlider.addEventListener(&#39;input&#39;, (e) =&gt; { const pop = sliderToPopulation(parseInt(e.target.value)); popInput.value = pop; clearTimeout(generateTimeout); generateTimeout = setTimeout(() =&gt; generatePopulation(), 300); });
popInput.addEventListener(&#39;input&#39;, (e) =&gt; { let pop = parseInt(e.target.value) || 1; pop = Math.max(1, Math.min(5000000, pop)); popSlider.value = populationToSlider(pop); clearTimeout(generateTimeout); generateTimeout = setTimeout(() =&gt; generatePopulation(), 500); });
popInput.addEventListener(&#39;blur&#39;, (e) =&gt; { let pop = parseInt(e.target.value) || 1; e.target.value = Math.max(1, Math.min(5000000, pop)); });
document.getElementById(&#39;regenerateBtn&#39;).addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; { baseSeed = parseInt(document.getElementById(&#39;seedInput&#39;).value) || 12345; generatePopulation(); });
document.getElementById(&#39;randomSeedBtn&#39;).addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, () =&gt; { baseSeed = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000); document.getElementById(&#39;seedInput&#39;).value = baseSeed; generatePopulation(); });
document.getElementById(&#39;modalOverlay&#39;).addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, (e) =&gt; { if (e.target === document.getElementById(&#39;modalOverlay&#39;)) closeModal(); });

baseSeed = parseInt(document.getElementById(&#39;seedInput&#39;).value) || 12345;
loadPhotos().then(() =&gt; generatePopulation());
